EXTRAORDINARY
(Published by Authority)
PART I : SECTION (I) — GENERAL
Government  Notifications
ThE SRI  LANkA   ARmED  SERvICES  LONG  SERvICE  mEDAL  
IT is hereby notified that His Excellency the President of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka and the Commander 
in Chief of the Armed Forces has been pleased to award to Sri Lanka Armed Services Long Service Medal to the Persons 
specified in the Schedule hereto.
By His Excellency’s Command,
 Eng.
 Karunasena HettiaracHcHi,
 Secretary,
 Ministry of Defence.
Colombo,
Ministry of Defence,
08th June, 2016.
